2020. 8. 8. 16:54, abyss오재 : # Review 1
Thankful for your kindly review,

for weakness,
- We also agree the need to design a novel algorithm of BOIL, but we think it is our future research topic, therefore we're working on progress.
- We compared with MAML only, since [1] proposed ANIL is similar to MAML, and we also validated that algorithm but we did not report the result because the result is really the same with the result of MAML. And, NIL is compared with our algorithm in Section 4.2.1.. Our algorithm weakly performs before adaptation, which means completely different from the working mechanism of MAML.
- Correct. This is the fundamental fact of MAML, which means the procedure of MAML is learned for extracting good representaions. "Rethinking Few-Shot Image Classification: a Good Embedding Is All You Need?" might be a great reference. Existing few-shot algorithms is based on a great representation learning, and hence the performance without classifier may acheive to some extent of our goal. However, we want to highlight the fact that our algorihm can be improved with classfier, which is different from MAML.
- …
- We reported time-complexity in the first paragraph in Section 3. Because we just change the learning rate for body, the time-complexity for BOIL is the same with MAML.
- … 

We want for you to recognize our algorithm as not just extension of MAML but a new algorithm, since the fundamental concept is completely different from MAML.
